    (38) while_stmt_open -> while_cond . open_stmt

    (40) simple_stmt -> . expr ;

    (36) for_stmt_closed -> . for_header closed_stmt
    (31) if_stmt_closed -> . if_cond closed_stmt ELSE closed_stmt
    (38) while_stmt_open -> . while_cond open_stmt
    (35) for_stmt_open -> . for_header open_stmt
    (32) if_stmt_open -> . if_cond closed_stmt ELSE if_stmt_open
    (33) if_stmt_open -> . if_cond stmt
    (58) expr -> . expr1
    (4) decl -> . decl_init
    (5) decl -> . class_decl
    (6) decl -> . ID : type_func ;
    (7) decl -> . ID : type_array_sized ;
    (8) decl -> . ID : type_simple ;
    (51) block_stmt -> . { stmt_list }

    (49) break_stmt -> . BREAK ;
    (48) return_stmt -> . RETURN opt_expr ;
    (47) print_stmt -> . PRINT opt_expr_list ;
    (37) while_cond -> . WHILE ( opt_expr )
    (34) for_header -> . FOR ( opt_expr ; opt_expr ; opt_expr )
    (30) if_cond -> . IF ( opt_expr )
    (59) expr1 -> . expr2
    (60) expr1 -> . lval MODEQ expr1
    (61) expr1 -> . lval DIVEQ expr1
    (62) expr1 -> . lval MULEQ expr1
    (63) expr1 -> . lval SUBEQ expr1
    (64) expr1 -> . lval ADDEQ expr1
    (65) expr1 -> . lval = expr1
    (9) decl_init -> . ID : type_func = { opt_stmt_list }
    (10) decl_init -> . ID : type_array_sized = { opt_expr_list } ;
    (11) decl_init -> . ID : CONSTANT = expr ;
    (12) decl_init -> . ID : type_simple = expr ;
    (13) class_decl -> . ID : CLASS = { class_body }
    (68) expr2 -> . expr3
    (69) expr2 -> . expr2 LOR expr3
    (66) lval -> . ID index

    (75) expr4 -> . expr4 LE expr5
    (76) expr4 -> . expr4 LT expr5
    (77) expr4 -> . expr4 NE expr5
    (78) expr4 -> . expr4 EQ expr5
    (79) expr5 -> . expr6
    (80) expr5 -> . expr5 - expr6
